{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01HdUjAtgNV59QhnAxP11iun","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t---\n2\tdoc_type: spec\n3\tstatus: active\n4\tworkstream: vk-swarm-design-system\n5\tchange_kind: behaviour\n6\t---\n7\t\n8\t# vk-swarm-design-system — Midnight Terminal component vocabulary + hive app UI kit\n9\t\n10\t> **Origin:** Claude Design handoff bundle, preserved verbatim at\n11\t> `dev-docs/designs/2026-07-04-vk-swarm-design-system/design-source/`. Design spec at\n12\t> `design-spec.md`; gap analysis at `gap-analysis.md` (31 findings: 1 A, 7 B, 23 C). Ingested via\n13\t> `/wai:design-handoff-ingest`.\n14\t>\n15\t> **Relationship to `vk-swarm-hive-ui`:** that workstream's phase 1 (tasks 100-106 — hive auth shell:\n16\t> ProfileProvider, oauthApi, useAuth, NormalLayout, AppRouter, root providers) is **reusable\n17\t> infrastructure** for this workstream's hive app UI kit. `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 2-3 (tasks 202-308,\n18\t> the verbatim shadcn-copy approach) is **superseded** — the design system replaces \"copy shadcn\n19\t> swarm components verbatim\" with a purpose-built `.vks-*` component vocabulary.\n20\t\n21\t## Intent (what / why)\n22\t\n23\tThe VK-Swarm product has a design language — \"Midnight Terminal\" — captured in a Claude Design\n24\thandoff bundle. The design specifies a complete `.vks-*` component-class vocabulary (buttons,\n25\tbadges, cards, inputs, switches, checkboxes, tabs, selects, loaders, task cards, node cards,\n26\tstatus badges, settings rows/sections), a refined token set (typography scale, spacing, radius,\n27\tmotion, glows, textures), and a hive app UI kit (BoardView, Chrome, Panels/TaskDrawer).\n28\t\n29\t**Today:**\n30\t- The **node frontend** (`frontend/`) already implements the brand palette (`--vks-*` color tokens\n31\t  at `frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76`), two texture utilities (`.vks-ansi-dither`,\n32\t  `.vks-scanlines` at `frontend/src/styles/index.css:9-12`), and feature components (kanban,\n33\t  TaskCard, StatusBadge, NodeCard) — but built on **shadcn/ui primitives + Tailwind utility\n34\t  classes**, NOT the `.vks-*` component classes the design specifies. The node frontend is the HA\n35\t  fallback and is NOT modified by this workstream.\n36\t- The **hive frontend** (`remote-frontend/`) has only the auth shell (tasks 100-106 from\n37\t  `vk-swarm-hive-ui`) — none of the design system, none of the app UI kit.\n38\t\n39\tThis workstream builds the design system in `remote-frontend/` and mounts the hive app UI kit on\n40\ttop of the existing auth shell. The node frontend is untouched (HA fallback).\n41\t\n42\t## Users / who is affected\n43\t\n44\t- **Operator/admin (browser):** the human who manages nodes, swarm projects, labels, templates,\n45\t  and views the cross-node task board. After this workstream they use a hive-hosted console with\n46\t  the Midnight Terminal design language — distinct from today's node-frontend shadcn UI.\n47\t- **End-user / coder (browser):** the human running coding agents on tasks. After this workstream\n48\t  they view tasks/attempts/executions across all nodes in one hive-hosted board (BoardView) with\n49\t  the TaskDrawer for per-task detail (diff/logs/attempts panels).\n50\t- **Node-frontend users:** unaffected. The node frontend keeps its shadcn/Tailwind UI as the\n51\t  always-on fallback during hive outage.\n52\t\n53\t## User stories\n54\t\n55\t- **US1:** As an operator, when I open the hive console, I expect to see a Midnight Terminal\n56\t  interface — dark void background, cyan primary actions, terminal-textured empty states — not\n57\t  the generic shadcn UI.\n58\t- **US2:** As an operator/end-user, when I open the hive console, I expect to see a 5-column\n59\t  kanban board (todo/inprogress/inreview/done/cancelled) with tasks from all connected nodes,\n60\t  each card showing status, node, labels, and attempt indicator.\n61\t- **US3:** As an end-user, when I click a task card, I expect a slide-in drawer (capped\n62\t  `min(460px, 90vw)`) with tabs for diff, logs, and attempts — console-styled panels with\n63\t  ANSI/BBS line coloring.\n64\t- **US4:** As an operator, when I view the nodes page, I expect a NodeCard grid\n65\t  (`repeat(auto-fill, minmax(320px, 1fr))`) with per-OS glyphs (mac/linux/windows) and online pulse\n66\t  indicators.\n67\t- **US5:** As an operator, when I sign into the hive console, I expect the existing auth shell\n68\t  (from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 1) wrapped in the Midnight Terminal chrome (Navbar with logo,\n69\t  theme toggle, nav tabs).\n70\t- **US6:** As an operator, during a hive outage, I expect the node frontend's existing UI to keep\n71\t  working as the HA fallback — the design system lands in the hive only, the node frontend is\n72\t  untouched.\n73\t\n74\t## Success criteria\n75\t\n76\t- **SC1:** The `.vks-*` component-class vocabulary is implemented in `remote-frontend/` — all\n77\t  classes from `design-source/tokens/components.css` (`.vks-btn`, `.vks-badge`, `.vks-card`,\n78\t  `.vks-input`, `.vks-switch`, `.vks-checkbox`, `.vks-tabs`, `.vks-select`, `.vks-loader`,\n79\t  `.vks-task`, `.vks-node`, `.vks-status`, `.vks-settings`, `.vks-field`, `.vks-alert`,\n80\t  `.vks-savebar`) with their hover/focus/active/disabled states. → US1\n81\t- **SC2:** The refined token set is implemented in `remote-frontend/` — typography scale\n82\t  (`--vks-text-xs`..`--vks-text-5xl`, base=14px), spacing (`--vks-space-1`..`--vks-space-16`, 4px\n83\t  grid), radius, motion keyframes (`vks-spin .7s`, `vks-pulse 2s`, switch thumb cubic-bezier),\n84\t  shadows, glows — per `design-source/tokens/{typography,spacing,base,components}.css`. → US1\n85\t- **SC3:** The texture utilities are implemented in `remote-frontend/` — `.vks-ansi-dither`,\n86\t  `.vks-ansi-weave`, `.vks-ansi-grid`, `.vks-scanlines`, `.vks-diagonal-lines`, `.vks-wordmark`,\n87\t  `.vks-eyebrow`, `.vks-dashed` per `design-source/tokens/base.css:40-134`. → US1\n88\t- **SC4:** Core React components are implemented in `remote-frontend/src/components/core/` —\n89\t  Button, Badge, Card, Input, Switch, Checkbox, Tabs, Select, Loader — each matching its\n90\t  `design-source/components/core/*.jsx` anatomy, variants, and props. → US1\n91\t- **SC5:** Board components are implemented in `remote-frontend/src/components/board/` — TaskCard\n92\t  (with 4px status strip + AttemptIndicator), NodeCard (with OS glyph + online pulse), StatusBadge\n93\t  (5 statuses) — each matching its `design-source/components/board/*.jsx` anatomy. → US2, US4\n94\t- **SC6:** Settings components are implemented in\n95\t  `remote-frontend/src/components/settings/` — SettingsSection, SettingsRow (stacked/inline/nested\n96\t  variants) — per `design-source/components/settings/*.jsx`. → US1\n97\t- **SC7:** The hive app UI kit is implemented in `remote-frontend/src/ui/` — BoardView (5-column\n98\t  kanban, ColumnHeader, horizontal scroll, `░▒ no tasks ▒░` empty state), Chrome (Navbar with logo,\n99\t  ThemeToggle, NavIcon, NavTab, useBreakpoint), Panels (NodesView NodeCard grid, ProcessesView,\n100\t  TaskDrawer with DiffPanel/LogsPanel/AttemptsPanel) — per\n101\t  `design-source/ui_kits/vk-swarm-app/*.jsx`. → US2, US3, US4, US5\n102\t- **SC8:** The hive app shell (from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 1, tasks 100-106) renders inside the\n103\t  Midnight Terminal chrome — the existing AppRouter/NormalLayout/Navbar is restyled or replaced\n104\t  with the design system's Chrome. → US5\n105\t- **SC9:** The node frontend (`frontend/`) is **unmodified** — no regression to the HA fallback.\n106\t  → US6\n107\t\n108\t## Constraints\n109\t\n110\t- **Keep:** the existing hive auth shell (tasks 100-106: ProfileProvider, oauthApi, useAuth,\n111\t  AppRouter, root providers). The design system wraps/replaces the slim NormalLayout/Navbar/\n112\t  BottomNav from task 104 with the design's Chrome.\n113\t- **No node-frontend modifications:** the node frontend is the HA fallback. The design system\n114\t  lands in `remote-frontend/` only. Existing `--vks-*` color tokens in\n115\t  `frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76` are NOT edited (they're the node frontend's own impl).\n116\t- **Design source is immutable:** `design-source/` is a preserved snapshot; no downstream step\n117\t  edits it. The design spec (`design-spec.md`) is the canonical reference.\n118\t- **Bare JSON API contract:** the hive returns bare `Json(...)` (no envelope) — established by\n119\t  `vk-swarm-hive-ui` tasks 101-102. New API clients in the design system follow the same pattern\n120\t  (`makeRequest` + `if (!response.ok) throw` + `response.json() as T`).\n121\t- **Bearer token auth:** `localStorage['access_token']` + `Authorization: Bearer` header —\n122\t  established by tasks 101-102. No cookie/session auth.\n123\t- **Routes nest under `/v1`:** `crates/remote/src/routes/mod.rs:112-113`. All API paths use the\n124\t  `/v1` prefix.\n125\t- **Fonts from Google Fonts:** Inter, JetBrains Mono, Source Serif 4, Chivo Mono — per\n126\t  `design-source/tokens/fonts.css`. Loaded via `@import` in CSS.\n127\t- **dark-first + light opt-in:** the design is dark-first; light mode is opt-in via a `.light`\n128\t  class on the root. Both themes must work.\n129\t- **GitHub targeting:** PRs only against `davidrudduck/vk-swarm`.\n130\t\n131\t## Out of scope\n132\t\n133\t- **Node-frontend restyle:** the node frontend keeps its shadcn/Tailwind UI. The `.vks-*` color\n134\t  tokens at `frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76` are NOT edited (they're the node frontend's\n135\t  own implementation; this workstream does not touch `frontend/`).\n136\t- **B-class fidelity fixes to node frontend** (gap-analysis findings 11, 12, 18, 19, 22, 23): the\n137\t  node frontend's NodeCard/StatusBadge/texture/font-token drift from the design is NOT fixed here —\n138\t  the node frontend is the HA fallback and is untouched. These are documented in `gap-analysis.md`\n139\t  for a future node-frontend restyle workstream.\n140\t- **A-class bug fixes** (gap-analysis finding 21: fonts): none — fonts already match.\n141\t- **Mobile/responsive beyond the design's spec:** the design specifies breakpoints (mobile <640,\n142\t  tablet 640-1023, desktop ≥1024) and hit targets (≥34px, 44px touch). This workstream implements\n143\t  those; no additional mobile work.\n144\t- **Protocol / data-plane work:** owned by `vk-swarm-hive-redesign` (shipped). This workstream\n145\t  consumes published Electric shapes; it does not alter the protocol.\n146\t- **Cross-node aggregation logic** (the Electric collections for `node_task_assignments`/\n147\t  `node_task_output_logs`/`node_task_progress_events`): that was `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3\n148\t  (tasks 300-308). This workstream renders the BoardView/TaskDrawer UI; the data wiring is a\n149\t  separate concern (may be a follow-up or folded in — see Approach).\n150\t- **Backend changes:** no server changes. All routes the UI needs already exist\n151\t  (`/v1/profile`, `/v1/oauth/web/*`, `/v1/nodes`, `/v1/swarm/*`, `/v1/tasks/*`,\n152\t  `/v1/api/electric/v1/shape`).\n153\t\n154\t## Approach\n155\t\n156\tThree phases, sequentially dependent:\n157\t\n158\t1. **Tokens + textures (foundation):** port the design tokens (colors, typography, spacing,\n159\t   radius, motion, shadows, glows) and texture utilities from `design-source/tokens/` into\n160\t   `remote-frontend/src/styles/tokens.css` (or split files). Reconcile with the existing\n161\t   `remote-frontend/src/index.css` (which currently has only `@tailwind base/components/utilities`).\n162\t   The token phase is the foundation — components and UI kit depend on it.\n163\t\n164\t2. **Core + board + settings components:** implement the React components in\n165\t   `remote-frontend/src/components/{core,board,settings}/` matching the `design-source/components/`\n166\t   JSX anatomy. Each component is a thin React wrapper over the `.vks-*` CSS classes from phase 1.\n167\t   Components are presentational (no data fetching); they take props and render. Tests verify\n168\t   structure + variants + states against the design source.\n169\t\n170\t3. **App UI kit + shell integration:** implement BoardView, Chrome, Panels/TaskDrawer in\n171\t   `remote-frontend/src/ui/` per `design-source/ui_kits/vk-swarm-app/*.jsx`. Replace the slim\n172\t   task-104 NormalLayout/Navbar/BottomNav with the design's Chrome. Mount BoardView at `/tasks`,\n173\t   NodesView at `/nodes` (replacing the placeholder), ProcessesView at `/processes`. The TaskDrawer\n174\t   renders on task card click. Data wiring (Electric collections + REST clients) is folded in here\n175\t   — the BoardView consumes task data; if the Electric collections from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3\n176\t   aren't built yet, BoardView uses REST via `@tanstack/react-query` as a fallback (the data plane\n177\t   exists; only the client collections are missing).\n178\t\n179\tPhases compose: phase 1 delivers the token foundation; phase 2 delivers the component vocabulary\n180\tthat phase 3's UI kit composes into screens.\n181\t\n182\t## Design / architecture\n183\t\n184\t### Token layer (phase 1)\n185\t\n186\t```\n187\tremote-frontend/src/styles/\n188\t├── index.css              # entry: @import tokens + base\n189\t├── tokens.css             # :root + .dark + .light — all --vks-* tokens\n190\t├── base.css               # element defaults + texture utilities (.vks-ansi-*, .vks-scanlines, etc.)\n191\t└── components.css         # .vks-btn, .vks-card, .vks-task, .vks-node, etc. (all component classes)\n192\t```\n193\t\n194\t**Token reconciliation:** the design's `colors.css` uses hex values; the node frontend's existing\n195\t`--vks-*` tokens (`frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76`) use HSL triplets. This workstream uses\n196\tthe design's hex values directly (via `#hex` or converted to HSL where the CSS architecture\n197\texpects HSL — decision deferred to the task). The node frontend's tokens are NOT edited.\n198\t\n199\t**Texture utilities:** ported verbatim from `design-source/tokens/base.css:40-134`. The two\n200\texisting utilities in `frontend/src/styles/index.css:9-12` (`.vks-ansi-dither`, `.vks-scanlines`)\n201\tare the reference pattern but are NOT edited — the hive gets its own copy.\n202\t\n203\t### Component layer (phase 2)\n204\t\n205\t```\n206\tremote-frontend/src/components/\n207\t├── core/\n208\t│   ├── Button.tsx         # variants: primary/secondary/outline/ghost/destructive/link; sizes: xs/sm/md/lg/icon\n209\t│   ├── Badge.tsx           # variants: default/secondary/destructive/outline; optional dot\n210\t│   ├── Card.tsx            # compound: Card > Header > {Title, Description} > Content > Footer\n211\t│   ├── Input.tsx           # optional mono prop\n212\t│   ├── Switch.tsx          # controlled/uncontrolled\n213\t│   ├── Checkbox.tsx        # controlled/uncontrolled\n214\t│   ├── Tabs.tsx            # segmented control\n215\t│   ├── Select.tsx          # native select styled\n216\t│   └── Loader.tsx          # spinner sm/md/lg\n217\t├── board/\n218\t│   ├── TaskCard.tsx        # 4px status strip + AttemptIndicator\n219\t│   ├── NodeCard.tsx        # OS glyph (mac/linux/windows) + online pulse\n220\t│   └── StatusBadge.tsx     # 5 statuses, dot + optional label\n221\t└── settings/\n222\t    ├── SettingsSection.tsx # Card with header + stacked body\n223\t    └── SettingsRow.tsx     # stacked/inline/nested variants\n224\t```\n225\t\n226\tEach component is a thin TS React wrapper over the `.vks-*` CSS classes. Props match the\n227\t`design-source/components/*/*.jsx` signatures (typed via the `.d.ts` siblings). No data fetching —\n228\tpresentational only.\n229\t\n230\t### App UI kit layer (phase 3)\n231\t\n232\t```\n233\tremote-frontend/src/ui/\n234\t├── BoardView.tsx           # 5-column kanban, ColumnHeader, horizontal scroll, empty state\n235\t├── Chrome.tsx              # Navbar (Logo + ThemeToggle + NavIcon + NavTab), useBreakpoint hook\n236\t├── NodesView.tsx           # NodeCard grid repeat(auto-fill, minmax(320px, 1fr))\n237\t├── ProcessesView.tsx       # loader + status + name + node + duration rows\n238\t├── TaskDrawer.tsx          # slide-in min(460px, 90vw), Tabs(diff/logs/attempts)\n239\t├── DiffPanel.tsx           # console bg, add/del/ctx/meta line classes\n240\t├── LogsPanel.tsx           # console bg, muted/ok/fg/cy/err line classes\n241\t└── AttemptsPanel.tsx       # attempt rows\n242\t```\n243\t\n244\t**Shell integration:** the existing `remote-frontend/src/components/layout/NormalLayout.tsx` (task\n245\t104, 15 lines) + `Navbar.tsx` (67 lines) + `BottomNav.tsx` (68 lines) are replaced by the design's\n246\tChrome. The `AppRouter.tsx` (task 105) keeps its route structure but the layout component changes.\n247\tProfileProvider + oauthApi + useAuth (tasks 101-103) stay — the Chrome's ThemeToggle reads/writes\n248\ta `.light`/`.dark` class on `document.documentElement`.\n249\t\n250\t**Data wiring:** BoardView consumes task data. The `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3 (Electric collections)\n251\tis superseded by this workstream — BoardView uses `@tanstack/react-query` against the hive's\n252\texisting REST routes (`/v1/tasks/bulk`, `/v1/tasks/by-source`) for the initial render, and may\n253\tsubscribe to the Electric proxy (`/v1/api/electric/v1/shape`) for live updates if the collections\n254\tare added. The REST-first approach is the fallback; Electric is the optimization. Decision: REST\n255\tfirst (the routes exist and are tested); Electric collections are a follow-up optimization, not a\n256\tblocker for the UI.\n257\t\n258\t### Decisions\n259\t\n260\t- **D1: Design system lands in `remote-frontend/` only, node frontend untouched.** The node\n261\t  frontend is the HA fallback; its existing `--vks-*` tokens and shadcn UI stay. This is reversible\n262\t  (the node frontend could be restyled later) but is treated as a constraint for this workstream.\n263\t  Not irreversible → no ADR.\n264\t- **D2: REST-first data wiring, Electric optional.** BoardView uses REST via react-query against\n265\t  existing `/v1/tasks/*` routes. Electric collections (the `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3 plan) are a\n266\t  follow-up optimization, not a blocker. Reversible → no ADR.\n267\t- **D3: Replace task-104 NormalLayout/Navbar/BottomNav with design's Chrome.** The slim shell from\n268\t  `vk-swarm-hive-ui` task 104 is replaced, not extended. The auth shell (tasks 101-103, 105-106)\n269\t  stays. Reversible (the task-104 files are in git history) → no ADR.\n270\t- **D4: Hex token values from design, not HSL triplets from node frontend.** The design's\n271\t  `colors.css` uses hex (`#1a1a33`); the node frontend uses HSL triplets (`240 20% 5%`). This\n272\t  workstream uses the design's values. The node frontend's tokens are NOT edited. Reversible →\n273\t  no ADR.\n274\t\n275\tNo irreversible decisions (no deletes, no migrations, no wire-format changes, no breaking\n276\trenames). All decisions are reversible in `remote-frontend/`.\n277\t\n278\t## Test strategy\n279\t\n280\t- **Unit tests** per component: render with each variant/prop/state, assert structure (class\n281\t  names, element hierarchy) matches the `design-source/components/*/*.jsx` anatomy. Use\n282\t  `@testing-library/react` (already installed by task 100).\n283\t- **Token tests:** assert each `--vks-*` token is defined in `:root` and resolves to the design's\n284\t  value. Compile-time + runtime (CSS is parsed, variables resolve).\n285\t- **Texture utility tests:** assert each `.vks-*` utility class produces the expected visual\n286\t  property (e.g. `.vks-scanlines::after` has `content: \"\"`).\n287\t- **Integration tests:** BoardView renders 5 columns with ColumnHeader; TaskDrawer opens on card\n288\t  click; Chrome renders Navbar with theme toggle; NodesView renders NodeCard grid.\n289\t- **Parity tests (SC9):** `cd frontend && npx tsc --noEmit` still passes (node frontend\n290\t  unmodified). The node frontend's `npm run lint` and `npm run build` still pass.\n291\t- **Visual smoke:** `cd remote-frontend && npm run build` exits 0 (Vite builds the design system +\n292\t  UI kit without errors)."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"9e99ba6e-4151-4031-a26e-3a11915b4a84","uuid":"f69dfdb5-4a23-40b1-9d78-6badb0a1c081","timestamp":"2026-07-04T14:15:38.319Z","tool_use_result":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"/home/david/.local/share/opencode/worktree/864023a7bea1094222edb02741f5b7e3b07c3f4d/hidden-sailor/docs/superpowers/specs/2026-07-04-vk-swarm-design-system.md","content":"---\ndoc_type: spec\nstatus: active\nworkstream: vk-swarm-design-system\nchange_kind: behaviour\n---\n\n# vk-swarm-design-system — Midnight Terminal component vocabulary + hive app UI kit\n\n> **Origin:** Claude Design handoff bundle, preserved verbatim at\n> `dev-docs/designs/2026-07-04-vk-swarm-design-system/design-source/`. Design spec at\n> `design-spec.md`; gap analysis at `gap-analysis.md` (31 findings: 1 A, 7 B, 23 C). Ingested via\n> `/wai:design-handoff-ingest`.\n>\n> **Relationship to `vk-swarm-hive-ui`:** that workstream's phase 1 (tasks 100-106 — hive auth shell:\n> ProfileProvider, oauthApi, useAuth, NormalLayout, AppRouter, root providers) is **reusable\n> infrastructure** for this workstream's hive app UI kit. `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 2-3 (tasks 202-308,\n> the verbatim shadcn-copy approach) is **superseded** — the design system replaces \"copy shadcn\n> swarm components verbatim\" with a purpose-built `.vks-*` component vocabulary.\n\n## Intent (what / why)\n\nThe VK-Swarm product has a design language — \"Midnight Terminal\" — captured in a Claude Design\nhandoff bundle. The design specifies a complete `.vks-*` component-class vocabulary (buttons,\nbadges, cards, inputs, switches, checkboxes, tabs, selects, loaders, task cards, node cards,\nstatus badges, settings rows/sections), a refined token set (typography scale, spacing, radius,\nmotion, glows, textures), and a hive app UI kit (BoardView, Chrome, Panels/TaskDrawer).\n\n**Today:**\n- The **node frontend** (`frontend/`) already implements the brand palette (`--vks-*` color tokens\n  at `frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76`), two texture utilities (`.vks-ansi-dither`,\n  `.vks-scanlines` at `frontend/src/styles/index.css:9-12`), and feature components (kanban,\n  TaskCard, StatusBadge, NodeCard) — but built on **shadcn/ui primitives + Tailwind utility\n  classes**, NOT the `.vks-*` component classes the design specifies. The node frontend is the HA\n  fallback and is NOT modified by this workstream.\n- The **hive frontend** (`remote-frontend/`) has only the auth shell (tasks 100-106 from\n  `vk-swarm-hive-ui`) — none of the design system, none of the app UI kit.\n\nThis workstream builds the design system in `remote-frontend/` and mounts the hive app UI kit on\ntop of the existing auth shell. The node frontend is untouched (HA fallback).\n\n## Users / who is affected\n\n- **Operator/admin (browser):** the human who manages nodes, swarm projects, labels, templates,\n  and views the cross-node task board. After this workstream they use a hive-hosted console with\n  the Midnight Terminal design language — distinct from today's node-frontend shadcn UI.\n- **End-user / coder (browser):** the human running coding agents on tasks. After this workstream\n  they view tasks/attempts/executions across all nodes in one hive-hosted board (BoardView) with\n  the TaskDrawer for per-task detail (diff/logs/attempts panels).\n- **Node-frontend users:** unaffected. The node frontend keeps its shadcn/Tailwind UI as the\n  always-on fallback during hive outage.\n\n## User stories\n\n- **US1:** As an operator, when I open the hive console, I expect to see a Midnight Terminal\n  interface — dark void background, cyan primary actions, terminal-textured empty states — not\n  the generic shadcn UI.\n- **US2:** As an operator/end-user, when I open the hive console, I expect to see a 5-column\n  kanban board (todo/inprogress/inreview/done/cancelled) with tasks from all connected nodes,\n  each card showing status, node, labels, and attempt indicator.\n- **US3:** As an end-user, when I click a task card, I expect a slide-in drawer (capped\n  `min(460px, 90vw)`) with tabs for diff, logs, and attempts — console-styled panels with\n  ANSI/BBS line coloring.\n- **US4:** As an operator, when I view the nodes page, I expect a NodeCard grid\n  (`repeat(auto-fill, minmax(320px, 1fr))`) with per-OS glyphs (mac/linux/windows) and online pulse\n  indicators.\n- **US5:** As an operator, when I sign into the hive console, I expect the existing auth shell\n  (from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 1) wrapped in the Midnight Terminal chrome (Navbar with logo,\n  theme toggle, nav tabs).\n- **US6:** As an operator, during a hive outage, I expect the node frontend's existing UI to keep\n  working as the HA fallback — the design system lands in the hive only, the node frontend is\n  untouched.\n\n## Success criteria\n\n- **SC1:** The `.vks-*` component-class vocabulary is implemented in `remote-frontend/` — all\n  classes from `design-source/tokens/components.css` (`.vks-btn`, `.vks-badge`, `.vks-card`,\n  `.vks-input`, `.vks-switch`, `.vks-checkbox`, `.vks-tabs`, `.vks-select`, `.vks-loader`,\n  `.vks-task`, `.vks-node`, `.vks-status`, `.vks-settings`, `.vks-field`, `.vks-alert`,\n  `.vks-savebar`) with their hover/focus/active/disabled states. → US1\n- **SC2:** The refined token set is implemented in `remote-frontend/` — typography scale\n  (`--vks-text-xs`..`--vks-text-5xl`, base=14px), spacing (`--vks-space-1`..`--vks-space-16`, 4px\n  grid), radius, motion keyframes (`vks-spin .7s`, `vks-pulse 2s`, switch thumb cubic-bezier),\n  shadows, glows — per `design-source/tokens/{typography,spacing,base,components}.css`. → US1\n- **SC3:** The texture utilities are implemented in `remote-frontend/` — `.vks-ansi-dither`,\n  `.vks-ansi-weave`, `.vks-ansi-grid`, `.vks-scanlines`, `.vks-diagonal-lines`, `.vks-wordmark`,\n  `.vks-eyebrow`, `.vks-dashed` per `design-source/tokens/base.css:40-134`. → US1\n- **SC4:** Core React components are implemented in `remote-frontend/src/components/core/` —\n  Button, Badge, Card, Input, Switch, Checkbox, Tabs, Select, Loader — each matching its\n  `design-source/components/core/*.jsx` anatomy, variants, and props. → US1\n- **SC5:** Board components are implemented in `remote-frontend/src/components/board/` — TaskCard\n  (with 4px status strip + AttemptIndicator), NodeCard (with OS glyph + online pulse), StatusBadge\n  (5 statuses) — each matching its `design-source/components/board/*.jsx` anatomy. → US2, US4\n- **SC6:** Settings components are implemented in\n  `remote-frontend/src/components/settings/` — SettingsSection, SettingsRow (stacked/inline/nested\n  variants) — per `design-source/components/settings/*.jsx`. → US1\n- **SC7:** The hive app UI kit is implemented in `remote-frontend/src/ui/` — BoardView (5-column\n  kanban, ColumnHeader, horizontal scroll, `░▒ no tasks ▒░` empty state), Chrome (Navbar with logo,\n  ThemeToggle, NavIcon, NavTab, useBreakpoint), Panels (NodesView NodeCard grid, ProcessesView,\n  TaskDrawer with DiffPanel/LogsPanel/AttemptsPanel) — per\n  `design-source/ui_kits/vk-swarm-app/*.jsx`. → US2, US3, US4, US5\n- **SC8:** The hive app shell (from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 1, tasks 100-106) renders inside the\n  Midnight Terminal chrome — the existing AppRouter/NormalLayout/Navbar is restyled or replaced\n  with the design system's Chrome. → US5\n- **SC9:** The node frontend (`frontend/`) is **unmodified** — no regression to the HA fallback.\n  → US6\n\n## Constraints\n\n- **Keep:** the existing hive auth shell (tasks 100-106: ProfileProvider, oauthApi, useAuth,\n  AppRouter, root providers). The design system wraps/replaces the slim NormalLayout/Navbar/\n  BottomNav from task 104 with the design's Chrome.\n- **No node-frontend modifications:** the node frontend is the HA fallback. The design system\n  lands in `remote-frontend/` only. Existing `--vks-*` color tokens in\n  `frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76` are NOT edited (they're the node frontend's own impl).\n- **Design source is immutable:** `design-source/` is a preserved snapshot; no downstream step\n  edits it. The design spec (`design-spec.md`) is the canonical reference.\n- **Bare JSON API contract:** the hive returns bare `Json(...)` (no envelope) — established by\n  `vk-swarm-hive-ui` tasks 101-102. New API clients in the design system follow the same pattern\n  (`makeRequest` + `if (!response.ok) throw` + `response.json() as T`).\n- **Bearer token auth:** `localStorage['access_token']` + `Authorization: Bearer` header —\n  established by tasks 101-102. No cookie/session auth.\n- **Routes nest under `/v1`:** `crates/remote/src/routes/mod.rs:112-113`. All API paths use the\n  `/v1` prefix.\n- **Fonts from Google Fonts:** Inter, JetBrains Mono, Source Serif 4, Chivo Mono — per\n  `design-source/tokens/fonts.css`. Loaded via `@import` in CSS.\n- **dark-first + light opt-in:** the design is dark-first; light mode is opt-in via a `.light`\n  class on the root. Both themes must work.\n- **GitHub targeting:** PRs only against `davidrudduck/vk-swarm`.\n\n## Out of scope\n\n- **Node-frontend restyle:** the node frontend keeps its shadcn/Tailwind UI. The `.vks-*` color\n  tokens at `frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76` are NOT edited (they're the node frontend's\n  own implementation; this workstream does not touch `frontend/`).\n- **B-class fidelity fixes to node frontend** (gap-analysis findings 11, 12, 18, 19, 22, 23): the\n  node frontend's NodeCard/StatusBadge/texture/font-token drift from the design is NOT fixed here —\n  the node frontend is the HA fallback and is untouched. These are documented in `gap-analysis.md`\n  for a future node-frontend restyle workstream.\n- **A-class bug fixes** (gap-analysis finding 21: fonts): none — fonts already match.\n- **Mobile/responsive beyond the design's spec:** the design specifies breakpoints (mobile <640,\n  tablet 640-1023, desktop ≥1024) and hit targets (≥34px, 44px touch). This workstream implements\n  those; no additional mobile work.\n- **Protocol / data-plane work:** owned by `vk-swarm-hive-redesign` (shipped). This workstream\n  consumes published Electric shapes; it does not alter the protocol.\n- **Cross-node aggregation logic** (the Electric collections for `node_task_assignments`/\n  `node_task_output_logs`/`node_task_progress_events`): that was `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3\n  (tasks 300-308). This workstream renders the BoardView/TaskDrawer UI; the data wiring is a\n  separate concern (may be a follow-up or folded in — see Approach).\n- **Backend changes:** no server changes. All routes the UI needs already exist\n  (`/v1/profile`, `/v1/oauth/web/*`, `/v1/nodes`, `/v1/swarm/*`, `/v1/tasks/*`,\n  `/v1/api/electric/v1/shape`).\n\n## Approach\n\nThree phases, sequentially dependent:\n\n1. **Tokens + textures (foundation):** port the design tokens (colors, typography, spacing,\n   radius, motion, shadows, glows) and texture utilities from `design-source/tokens/` into\n   `remote-frontend/src/styles/tokens.css` (or split files). Reconcile with the existing\n   `remote-frontend/src/index.css` (which currently has only `@tailwind base/components/utilities`).\n   The token phase is the foundation — components and UI kit depend on it.\n\n2. **Core + board + settings components:** implement the React components in\n   `remote-frontend/src/components/{core,board,settings}/` matching the `design-source/components/`\n   JSX anatomy. Each component is a thin React wrapper over the `.vks-*` CSS classes from phase 1.\n   Components are presentational (no data fetching); they take props and render. Tests verify\n   structure + variants + states against the design source.\n\n3. **App UI kit + shell integration:** implement BoardView, Chrome, Panels/TaskDrawer in\n   `remote-frontend/src/ui/` per `design-source/ui_kits/vk-swarm-app/*.jsx`. Replace the slim\n   task-104 NormalLayout/Navbar/BottomNav with the design's Chrome. Mount BoardView at `/tasks`,\n   NodesView at `/nodes` (replacing the placeholder), ProcessesView at `/processes`. The TaskDrawer\n   renders on task card click. Data wiring (Electric collections + REST clients) is folded in here\n   — the BoardView consumes task data; if the Electric collections from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3\n   aren't built yet, BoardView uses REST via `@tanstack/react-query` as a fallback (the data plane\n   exists; only the client collections are missing).\n\nPhases compose: phase 1 delivers the token foundation; phase 2 delivers the component vocabulary\nthat phase 3's UI kit composes into screens.\n\n## Design / architecture\n\n### Token layer (phase 1)\n\n```\nremote-frontend/src/styles/\n├── index.css              # entry: @import tokens + base\n├── tokens.css             # :root + .dark + .light — all --vks-* tokens\n├── base.css               # element defaults + texture utilities (.vks-ansi-*, .vks-scanlines, etc.)\n└── components.css         # .vks-btn, .vks-card, .vks-task, .vks-node, etc. (all component classes)\n```\n\n**Token reconciliation:** the design's `colors.css` uses hex values; the node frontend's existing\n`--vks-*` tokens (`frontend/src/styles/index.css:64-76`) use HSL triplets. This workstream uses\nthe design's hex values directly (via `#hex` or converted to HSL where the CSS architecture\nexpects HSL — decision deferred to the task). The node frontend's tokens are NOT edited.\n\n**Texture utilities:** ported verbatim from `design-source/tokens/base.css:40-134`. The two\nexisting utilities in `frontend/src/styles/index.css:9-12` (`.vks-ansi-dither`, `.vks-scanlines`)\nare the reference pattern but are NOT edited — the hive gets its own copy.\n\n### Component layer (phase 2)\n\n```\nremote-frontend/src/components/\n├── core/\n│   ├── Button.tsx         # variants: primary/secondary/outline/ghost/destructive/link; sizes: xs/sm/md/lg/icon\n│   ├── Badge.tsx           # variants: default/secondary/destructive/outline; optional dot\n│   ├── Card.tsx            # compound: Card > Header > {Title, Description} > Content > Footer\n│   ├── Input.tsx           # optional mono prop\n│   ├── Switch.tsx          # controlled/uncontrolled\n│   ├── Checkbox.tsx        # controlled/uncontrolled\n│   ├── Tabs.tsx            # segmented control\n│   ├── Select.tsx          # native select styled\n│   └── Loader.tsx          # spinner sm/md/lg\n├── board/\n│   ├── TaskCard.tsx        # 4px status strip + AttemptIndicator\n│   ├── NodeCard.tsx        # OS glyph (mac/linux/windows) + online pulse\n│   └── StatusBadge.tsx     # 5 statuses, dot + optional label\n└── settings/\n    ├── SettingsSection.tsx # Card with header + stacked body\n    └── SettingsRow.tsx     # stacked/inline/nested variants\n```\n\nEach component is a thin TS React wrapper over the `.vks-*` CSS classes. Props match the\n`design-source/components/*/*.jsx` signatures (typed via the `.d.ts` siblings). No data fetching —\npresentational only.\n\n### App UI kit layer (phase 3)\n\n```\nremote-frontend/src/ui/\n├── BoardView.tsx           # 5-column kanban, ColumnHeader, horizontal scroll, empty state\n├── Chrome.tsx              # Navbar (Logo + ThemeToggle + NavIcon + NavTab), useBreakpoint hook\n├── NodesView.tsx           # NodeCard grid repeat(auto-fill, minmax(320px, 1fr))\n├── ProcessesView.tsx       # loader + status + name + node + duration rows\n├── TaskDrawer.tsx          # slide-in min(460px, 90vw), Tabs(diff/logs/attempts)\n├── DiffPanel.tsx           # console bg, add/del/ctx/meta line classes\n├── LogsPanel.tsx           # console bg, muted/ok/fg/cy/err line classes\n└── AttemptsPanel.tsx       # attempt rows\n```\n\n**Shell integration:** the existing `remote-frontend/src/components/layout/NormalLayout.tsx` (task\n104, 15 lines) + `Navbar.tsx` (67 lines) + `BottomNav.tsx` (68 lines) are replaced by the design's\nChrome. The `AppRouter.tsx` (task 105) keeps its route structure but the layout component changes.\nProfileProvider + oauthApi + useAuth (tasks 101-103) stay — the Chrome's ThemeToggle reads/writes\na `.light`/`.dark` class on `document.documentElement`.\n\n**Data wiring:** BoardView consumes task data. The `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3 (Electric collections)\nis superseded by this workstream — BoardView uses `@tanstack/react-query` against the hive's\nexisting REST routes (`/v1/tasks/bulk`, `/v1/tasks/by-source`) for the initial render, and may\nsubscribe to the Electric proxy (`/v1/api/electric/v1/shape`) for live updates if the collections\nare added. The REST-first approach is the fallback; Electric is the optimization. Decision: REST\nfirst (the routes exist and are tested); Electric collections are a follow-up optimization, not a\nblocker for the UI.\n\n### Decisions\n\n- **D1: Design system lands in `remote-frontend/` only, node frontend untouched.** The node\n  frontend is the HA fallback; its existing `--vks-*` tokens and shadcn UI stay. This is reversible\n  (the node frontend could be restyled later) but is treated as a constraint for this workstream.\n  Not irreversible → no ADR.\n- **D2: REST-first data wiring, Electric optional.** BoardView uses REST via react-query against\n  existing `/v1/tasks/*` routes. Electric collections (the `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 3 plan) are a\n  follow-up optimization, not a blocker. Reversible → no ADR.\n- **D3: Replace task-104 NormalLayout/Navbar/BottomNav with design's Chrome.** The slim shell from\n  `vk-swarm-hive-ui` task 104 is replaced, not extended. The auth shell (tasks 101-103, 105-106)\n  stays. Reversible (the task-104 files are in git history) → no ADR.\n- **D4: Hex token values from design, not HSL triplets from node frontend.** The design's\n  `colors.css` uses hex (`#1a1a33`); the node frontend uses HSL triplets (`240 20% 5%`). This\n  workstream uses the design's values. The node frontend's tokens are NOT edited. Reversible →\n  no ADR.\n\nNo irreversible decisions (no deletes, no migrations, no wire-format changes, no breaking\nrenames). All decisions are reversible in `remote-frontend/`.\n\n## Test strategy\n\n- **Unit tests** per component: render with each variant/prop/state, assert structure (class\n  names, element hierarchy) matches the `design-source/components/*/*.jsx` anatomy. Use\n  `@testing-library/react` (already installed by task 100).\n- **Token tests:** assert each `--vks-*` token is defined in `:root` and resolves to the design's\n  value. Compile-time + runtime (CSS is parsed, variables resolve).\n- **Texture utility tests:** assert each `.vks-*` utility class produces the expected visual\n  property (e.g. `.vks-scanlines::after` has `content: \"\"`).\n- **Integration tests:** BoardView renders 5 columns with ColumnHeader; TaskDrawer opens on card\n  click; Chrome renders Navbar with theme toggle; NodesView renders NodeCard grid.\n- **Parity tests (SC9):** `cd frontend && npx tsc --noEmit` still passes (node frontend\n  unmodified). The node frontend's `npm run lint` and `npm run build` still pass.\n- **Visual smoke:** `cd remote-frontend && npm run build` exits 0 (Vite builds the design system +\n  UI kit without errors).","numLines":292,"startLine":1,"totalLines":292}}}

The design bundle (`dev-docs/designs/.../design-source/`) specifies a complete Midnight Terminal design system: a CSS-token layer (color/typography/spacing/radius/motion/texture), a set of class-based component primitives (`.vks-*`), 9 core + 3 board + 2 settings React components, and an app UI kit (BoardView/Chrome/TaskDrawer/Panels) that wires those components to live data. The gap analysis (`dev-docs/designs/.../gap-analysis.md`) classified 31 findings: 1 A, 7 B, 23 C — i.e. almost everything is un-built in `remote-frontend/`, while the node `frontend/` already carries a partial token subset (11 `--vks-*` colors, 2 texture utilities, Tailwind `vks.*` namespace) that must NOT be touched (SC9).\n10\t\n11\tThis plan ports the design system into the hive `remote-frontend/` only. The approach is strictly layered so each phase is independently shippable: tokens → components → app UI kit + shell integration. The token CSS files are copied byte-identical from the preserved `design-source/tokens/` (the `.prettierignore` pattern established in task 201 applies — generated/preserved files must not be reformatted). React components are TypeScript ports of the JSX siblings in `design-source/components/{core,board,settings}/` and `design-source/ui_kits/vk-swarm-app/` — the JSX files are the authoritative anatomy; the port translates `className` string composition to `cn()` (already in `remote-frontend/src/lib/utils.ts` from task 104), adds explicit prop types from the `.d.ts` siblings, and keeps the `vks-*` class names verbatim. The app UI kit (phase 3) wires the components to the live REST + Electric data planes already available in `remote-frontend/` (from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 1): `ProfileProvider`/`useAuth` for session, `nodesApi`-equivalent clients to be added against the hive `/v1/*` routes, and the Electric collections (existing 3 + new 3 from the abandoned tasks 300-308 — but only the 3 that are actually synced to Electric per `frontend/src/lib/electric/config.ts`'s `ELECTRIC_SHAPE_TABLES`: nodes, projects, node_projects, node_task_assignments, node_task_output_logs, node_task_progress_events). Phase 3 also integrates the new UI kit into the existing `AppRouter.tsx` route tree, replacing the slim task-104 `NormalLayout`/`Navbar`/`BottomNav` with the design-system `Chrome`, and swapping the `/nodes` and `/tasks` placeholders for `NodesView` and `BoardView`/`TaskDrawer` respectively.\n12\t\n13\tSC9 (node frontend unmodified) is enforced mechanically: every task's Done-when gate chains `cd frontend && npx tsc --noEmit` (the node frontend typecheck) so any accidental edit is caught. No task touches `frontend/`.\n14\t\n15\t## Phases\n16\t\n17\t### Phase 1 — Tokens & textures (SC2, SC3)\n18\t\n19\tCopy the 6 token CSS files + `base.css` texture utilities into `remote-frontend/src/styles/tokens/`, wire them into the existing `remote-frontend/src/index.css` entry, add a token-resolution unit test, and add a texture-utility DOM test. The node frontend's partial token set is NOT reconciled (out of scope, gap-analysis B-22; SC9). The design bundle (`dev-docs/designs/.../design-source/`) specifies a complete Midnight Terminal design system: a CSS-token layer (color/typography/spacing/radius/motion/texture), a set of class-based component primitives (`.vks-*`), 9 core + 3 board + 2 settings React components, and an app UI kit (BoardView/Chrome/TaskDrawer/Panels) that wires those components to live data. The gap analysis (`dev-docs/designs/.../gap-analysis.md`) classified 31 findings: 1 A, 7 B, 23 C — i.e. almost everything is un-built in `remote-frontend/`, while the node `frontend/` already carries a partial token subset (11 `--vks-*` colors, 2 texture utilities, Tailwind `vks.*` namespace) that must NOT be touched (SC9).\n\nThis plan ports the design system into the hive `remote-frontend/` only. The approach is strictly layered so each phase is independently shippable: tokens → components → app UI kit + shell integration. The token CSS files are copied byte-identical from the preserved `design-source/tokens/` (the `.prettierignore` pattern established in task 201 applies — generated/preserved files must not be reformatted). React components are TypeScript ports of the JSX siblings in `design-source/components/{core,board,settings}/` and `design-source/ui_kits/vk-swarm-app/` — the JSX files are the authoritative anatomy; the port translates `className` string composition to `cn()` (already in `remote-frontend/src/lib/utils.ts` from task 104), adds explicit prop types from the `.d.ts` siblings, and keeps the `vks-*` class names verbatim. The app UI kit (phase 3) wires the components to the live REST + Electric data planes already available in `remote-frontend/` (from `vk-swarm-hive-ui` phase 1): `ProfileProvider`/`useAuth` for session, `nodesApi`-equivalent clients to be added against the hive `/v1/*` routes, and the Electric collections (existing 3 + new 3 from the abandoned tasks 300-308 — but only the 3 that are actually synced to Electric per `frontend/src/lib/electric/config.ts`'s `ELECTRIC_SHAPE_TABLES`: nodes, projects, node_projects, node_task_assignments, node_task_output_logs, node_task_progress_events). Phase 3 also integrates the new UI kit into the existing `AppRouter.tsx` route tree, replacing the slim task-104 `NormalLayout`/`Navbar`/`BottomNav` with the design-system `Chrome`, and swapping the `/nodes` and `/tasks` placeholders for `NodesView` and `BoardView`/`TaskDrawer` respectively.\n\nSC9 (node frontend unmodified) is enforced mechanically: every task's Done-when gate chains `cd frontend && npx tsc --noEmit` (the node frontend typecheck) so any accidental edit is caught. No task touches `frontend/`.\n\n## Phases\n\n### Phase 1 — Tokens & textures (SC2, SC3)\n\nCopy the 6 token CSS files + `base.css` texture utilities into `remote-frontend/src/styles/tokens/`, wire them into the existing `remote-frontend/src/index.css` entry, add a token-resolution unit test, and add a texture-utility DOM test. The node frontend's partial token set is NOT reconciled (out of scope, gap-analysis B-22; SC9). The component signature:\n\n```ts\nimport { ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';\nimport { cn } from '@/lib/utils';\n\nexport type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'destructive' | 'link';\nexport type ButtonSize = 'xs' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'icon';\n\nconst SIZES: Record<ButtonSize, string> = { xs: 'vks-btn--xs', sm: 'vks-btn--sm', md: 'vks-btn--md', lg: 'vks-btn--lg', icon: 'vks-btn--icon' };\nconst VARIANTS: Record<ButtonVariant, string> = { primary: 'vks-btn--primary', secondary: 'vks-btn--secondary', outline: 'vks-btn--outline', ghost: 'vks-btn--ghost', destructive: 'vks-btn--destructive', link: 'vks-btn--link' };\n\nexport interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {\n  variant?: ButtonVariant;\n  size?: ButtonSize;\n}\n\nexport function Button({ variant = 'primary', size = 'md', className, children, ...props }: ButtonProps) {\n  const cls = cn('vks-btn', VARIANTS[variant] ?? VARIANTS.primary, SIZES[size] ?? SIZES.md, className);\n  return <button className={cls} {...props}>{children}</button>;\n}\n```\n\n### File: `remote-frontend/src/components/core/Badge.tsx` (CREATE)\nTypeScript port of `design-source/components/core/Badge.jsx` (19 lines). `BadgeVariant = 'default' | 'secondary' | 'destructive' | 'outline'`. } from 'react';\n114\t\n115\texport type Breakpoint = 'mobile' | 'tablet' | 'desktop';\n116\t\n117\texport function useBreakpoint(): Breakpoint {\n118\t  const get = () => (typeof window === 'undefined' ? 'desktop'\n119\t    : window.innerWidth < 640 ? 'mobile'\n120\t    : window.innerWidth < 1024 ? 'tablet' : 'desktop');\n121\t  const [bp, setBp] = useState<Breakpoint>(get);\n122\t  useEffect(() => {\n123\t    const on = () => setBp(get());\n124\t    window.addEventListener('resize', on);\n125\t    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', on);\n126\t  }, []);\n127\t  return bp;\n128\t}\n129\t```\n130\t\n131\t### File: `remote-frontend/src/app/chrome/Chrome.tsx` (CREATE)\n132\tTypeScript port of `Logo`, `ThemeToggle`, `Navbar`, `NavIcon`, `NavTab` from `chrome.jsx`. 'mobile' | 'tablet' | 'desktop';\n\nexport function useBreakpoint(): Breakpoint {\n  const get = () => (typeof window === 'undefined' ? 'desktop'\n    : window.innerWidth < 640 ? 'mobile'\n    : window.innerWidth < 1024 ? 'tablet' : 'desktop');\n  const [bp, setBp] = useState<Breakpoint>(get);\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const on = () => setBp(get());\n    window.addEventListener('resize', on);\n    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', on);\n  }, []);\n  return bp;\n}\n```\n\n### File: `remote-frontend/src/app/chrome/Chrome.tsx` (CREATE)\nTypeScript port of `Logo`, `ThemeToggle`, `Navbar`, `NavIcon`, `NavTab` from `chrome.jsx`.
